Conversation of the Director of the East Asia Bureau of Japan, Mr. Kuwashima, After Arriving in Beiping

Acknowledges the Puppet Organization of Eastern Hebei Should be Abolished, But Claims Japan Has No Intention of Invading China

Beiping Correspondence: Kuwashima Kazue, Director of the East Asia Bureau of the Japanese Foreign Ministry, arrived in Beiping from Tianjin on the evening of the 13th and stayed at Room 108 of the Beijing Hotel. At noon on the 14th, Song Zheyuan, Chairman of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, hosted a banquet at the Nanhai Hotel in the Summer Palace specifically to entertain Kuwashima, as well as former Japanese Vice Chief of Staff Sugiyama Gen, Chief of Staff of the Tianjin Japanese Garrison Headquarters Nagami Toshitoku, Matsumuro Takayoshi attached to the Garrison Headquarters, and invited Qin Dechun, Zhang Zizhong, Wang Yitang, Feng Zhi’an, Liu Ruming, and other military and political figures to attend. The banquet ended around 2 o'clock, followed by a garden tour. Around 3 o'clock, they returned to the city one after another. Nagami returned to Tianjin at 5 pm that afternoon. Kuwashima was scheduled to formally meet with Mr. Song on the 15th to discuss everything. On the morning of the 16th, he will go to Zhangjiakou for inspection and return to Beiping that evening. On the 17th, he will go to Jinan and Qingdao to visit Han Fuju, Shen Honglie, and others separately, and then go to Nanjing and Shanghai to visit important figures of our government. After finishing these matters, he will take a ship back to Japan from Shanghai. A reporter visited Kuwashima at the Beijing Hotel at 9:30 am on the 14th, and they talked for about an hour. Here is a record of his conversation: "I previously worked in Tianjin (as the Japanese Consul-General) for two and a half years. Later, I was transferred back to Japan to work in the Foreign Ministry, still handling East Asian affairs. However, due to the heavy workload, I was unable to leave my post, so it has been three full years since I last came to China. In these two years, China has undergone many changes, and the situation is also very different. This visit to China is to see the Chinese situation, what changes have occurred, to serve as a reference for future work. The places I plan to visit this time are Hebei, Tianjin, Beiping, Zhangjiakou, Jinan, Qingdao, Nanjing, and Shanghai. After completing the inspection, I will return to Japan.

After arriving in Tianjin, I met with Commander Tashiro, Chief of Staff Nagami, personnel from the Tianjin Japanese Consulate General, and old Chinese friends in Tianjin. The talks mostly revolved around the recent situation in Hebei. In Beiping, I also hope to have time to meet more people. The more people I meet, the more opinions I will hear. I will probably meet with Chairman Song formally on the 15th. As for the North China situation, to what extent it should reach, and how it can be resolved, because I have only met with a portion of friends, and have not yet met with members of the Political Council, I have no opinion to express at this time. I am very sorry. However, I believe that not only North China, but also the Chinese government should strive for the happiness of the people and the stability of people's lives. When the Japanese government works for this kind of thing for the Chinese government, it will definitely be able to provide assistance. I also believe that Sino-Japanese diplomacy should also take striving for the happiness of the people and the stability of people's lives as the standard. This is my general impression of North China. When I obtain more detailed information in the future, I will have more specific opinions.

Based on the above, it seems a bit abstract and empty. However, when I was working in Tianjin, I had this kind of feeling. For example, Hebei is a cotton-producing area, and Japanese spinning mills need a lot of this raw material, which has always come from England, the United States, and Egypt, precisely because the Chinese cotton seeds are not good. China and Japan are neighboring countries. If China improves its cotton seeds, then Japan should purchase them. This will also greatly help the stability of people's lives. Japan can also provide assistance economically. Now, China already has slogans like 'Plant Cotton to Save the Country,' and it is said that China is currently exporting cotton. Japan also uses it. This is really a good phenomenon. Another example is Shanxi, a province with inconvenient water conservancy. If water conservancy can be developed, agricultural production can naturally be developed. When I was in Manchuria, there was a well-drilling engineer named Shimizu. At the invitation of Mr. Yan Xishan, I introduced him to work there. Now, I hear that 300 wells have already been dug in Shanxi. This is of great benefit to the farmers of Shanxi, and Japan also benefits from it.

As for North China's diplomacy, because North China is a region of China, in principle, it should be handled by the Chinese government. However, because the Japanese side's understanding of North China is slightly different from that of the Chinese government, there is no difference between the Japanese military and diplomatic officials regarding North China policy. The Japanese government has a consistent policy, using this policy to deal with the situation in North China. Although North China has a special situation, the purpose of handling diplomacy is the same. It is not necessary to divide responsibility between the Foreign Ministry or the military. The North China region is special and changes very quickly. If the central government has a solution, the situation would not be as it is now. Therefore, this responsibility lies with the Chinese authorities."

When Kuwashima said this, the reporter asked what was special about the special situation he was referring to in North China. Kuwashima said, "Because I don't have time for a long talk, I will simply say that Japan is currently undertaking the defense responsibility of 'Manchukuo' and is responsible for the political, cultural, and economic development of 'Manchukuo.' The border between 'Manchukuo' and China is North China. Therefore, the special situation lies in this."

The reporter further inquired about the Eastern Hebei issue, asking if a resolution was possible. Kuwashima said, "Regarding this matter, I will only express my personal opinion. The Eastern Hebei organization should, in principle, merge with the Hebei-Chahar Political Council and should be abolished. It cannot exist permanently." However, when it can merge and to what extent it can be abolished is still under study and cannot be announced at this time. I believe that the Japanese increase in the North China garrison has no intention of invading China. Talking about adjusting the relationship between China and Japan, this is a very important issue. The two countries are studying it at all times. I believe that the relationship between the two countries must be adjusted, and it will definitely be adjusted. Now, I would like to hear everyone's high opinions on adjusting the relationship." The reporter stated that we, the people of the whole country, have many opinions on adjusting Sino-Japanese relations. Due to time constraints, I will only offer one of the most important points for reference, which is the hope that all issues between China and Japan should be resolved through diplomatic channels and legal procedures, to achieve genuine Sino-Japanese amity and cooperation. If force is resorted to, it will not be easy to completely conquer China with its vast territory and large population. Kuwashima expressed his agreement to this, saying that he is willing to work together and understand each other on the principle of taking into account the position and facts of both sides (14th).

Mr. Zhang Taiyan's Grand Funeral Today

The Funeral Ceremony Will Follow the Old Style Completely

Mr. Zhang Taiyan, a master of Chinese studies, passed away at his residence in Suzhou at approximately 8:00 AM on the 14th. Ding Weifen, a Central Committee member, came to Suzhou from Nanjing specifically to assist with the funeral arrangements. A funeral affairs office was organized, divided into five sections: general affairs, documentation, arrangement, accounting, and reception. Li Genyuan, Qian Zichu, Shen Junmin, Gong Zhenpeng, Deng Mengshuo, Zhang Ji, Ding Weifen, and Sha Pingxi were appointed as heads of general affairs; Sun Yingruo, Chu Zushuo, Xu Shifu, Pan Jingzheng, Huangfu Rongsheng, and Wang Peizheng were appointed as heads of documentation; Qian Jingfu, Ma Kuankuan, Hui Xin Ke, and Zheng Lichun were appointed as heads of arrangement; Sha Pingxi, Zhuang Ruiqing, Zheng Lichun, and Wang Chenglu were appointed as heads of accounting and general services; Nie Dezhao, Pan Xuanqing, Xu Yunqiu, Hui Xin Ke, Jin Donglei, Dai Jingcheng, Shi Chuncheng, Wang Qingzai, Wu Deyi, Bei Zhongqi, Zhu Suhai, Wang Peizheng, and Li Jiye were appointed as heads of reception. Telegrams announcing the passing were sent to various places, including Beiping, Tianjin, Nanjing, and Shanghai. The minor coffin ceremony was scheduled for 4:00 PM on the 15th, and the grand coffin ceremony for the 16th. The coffin is made of Phoebe zhennan wood, valued at 1,000 yuan. The grand coffin ceremony will follow the old style, according to the wishes of his wife, Tang Guoli. The hall arrangement is also in the old style. The Central Party Headquarters has allocated 3,000 yuan for funeral expenses and sent a telegram of condolence. Zhang Ji, a Central Committee member, flew to Suzhou from Xi'an on the afternoon of the 15th. Duan Qirui will also come to Suzhou to offer condolences. Important figures from the Central government will also come to Suzhou today (the 16th). Therefore, the funeral affairs office has set up a reception center at the New Suzhou Hotel and has dispatched personnel to the train station and other places to receive guests. After the arrival of important figures from various parties, memorial service arrangements will be discussed. Yu Youren, President of the Control Yuan, specially dispatched his representative, Supervisor Zeng Tongyi, from Nanjing to Suzhou on the 15th to offer condolences. The planned coffin ceremony includes: (1) playing mourning music; (2) offering condolences; (3) playing ceremonial music; (4) presenting formal attire; (5) playing mourning music; (6) raising the cover; (7) tying the knots; (8) raising the coffin; (9) playing mourning music; (10) presenting the burial items; (11) leveling; (12) dividing the gold; (13) offering wine; (14) food offering; (15) playing mourning music; (16) adding a veil; (17) adding the lid. Excerpts from condolence telegrams from various parties are as follows: (1) Feng Yuxiang's telegram: "To Madam Zhang and her descendants, upon hearing the news of Mr. Taiyan's passing, my grief knows no bounds. Mr. Taiyan's literary talent and morality were unparalleled in his time. He discussed the past and present to guide future scholars. I had hoped that his occasional ailments would pass and that he would recover his health to jointly reverse the declining trends. How could I have imagined that such terrible news would arrive and he would return to the mountains. Cherishing his bright virtue, my heart is filled with sorrow. I hope that Madam and others will restrain their sorrow to assist in the important affairs. I send my condolences in advance." (2) Ju Zheng's telegram: "To Madam Zhang and her sons, upon hearing of the death of the Grand Master, without any prior knowledge of illness, I am deeply saddened by this sudden loss. It is like the collapse of a mountain. I pray that you will raise and nurture the successors. Restrain your grief and accept the changes to comfort his soul in heaven." (3) Li Liejun's telegram: "To Madam Zhang and her descendants, I am shocked to learn of Mr. Zhang's passing. Looking towards Suzhou, my pain knows no bounds. Mr. Zhang was both a teacher of scriptures and a teacher of men, a model for the world. His sudden passing leaves the masses without guidance. Liejun feels deeply affected in both public and private matters, and his loss is immeasurable. The feeling of the loss of a great man is extraordinary. I hope that his virtue and countenance will be spread through hundreds of rituals, which may also comfort him in the afterlife. I hope you will restrain your sorrow to assist in the important affairs. Tears fall in the wind, I send my deepest condolences." (4) Zhang Ji, Liu Shoushou, and Liu, telegram: "To Madam Zhang, we are shocked to hear that Mr. Taiyan has returned to the mountains so suddenly. It is a misfortune for the country and a loss of civilization. The terrible news has left us speechless. We hope that you will act with respect and affection, and together with your virtuous sons, mourn with sincerity. I will definitely arrive tomorrow to assist in the affairs." (5) Bo Wenwei's telegram: "To Madam Zhang and her sons, upon receiving the telegram of mourning, I am shocked to learn of Mr. Taiyan's sudden passing. My sorrow knows no bounds. At this time of national crisis, people are dying and the country is withering. Looking towards Wu, there are no tears left to shed. I pray that you will adapt to the situation and restrain your grief to assist in the important affairs. This is my deepest prayer." (6) Telegram from Qian Xuantong, Wu Chengshi, Xu Shoushang, Ma Yuzhao, Zhou Zuoren, Shen Jianshi, etc., in Beiping: "To Brother Zhang Mengkuangzhonglian, We are deeply saddened by the passing of our teacher. We send our respects." Attached is an image inscription written by Shen Zumin: "This is an image of my deceased friend, Mr. Taiyan. I am deeply saddened upon seeing it. I look upon his face, untouched by a speck of dust. Mr. Taiyan's aspirations are the same as those of Tinglin, Chuanshan, and Lizhou, and he is even more learned. Mr. Taiyan's achievements can only be compared to Zifang, Marquis Wu, and Qingtian. He did not fulfill his talent. He was born at the wrong time, and his fate was doomed. Sighing at himself, the stars offended Doukui. The beams of wood are in his heart, and Mount Tai is collapsing. Your humble brother, Shen Zumin, bows and inscribes with tears." As for the "Zhiyan Half-Monthly" (制言) magazine founded by the master, it will continue to be published by his disciples.

Zhejiang Aquatic Products Experiment Station Requests the Establishment of Aquatic Product Refrigeration and Transportation

Planning to Establish Four More Refrigeration Warehouses

Utilizing Railroads to Transport and Sell Fish

Annual Profit of 40,000 Yuan Possible

Dinghai Correspondence: Since its establishment, the Zhejiang Provincial Aquatic Products Experiment Station has spared no effort in developing and improving basic fisheries work. To promote fisheries construction, increase coastal fisheries production, expand fish sales, and seek exchange of Zhejiang and Jiangxi specialties and economic cooperation, a detailed plan has been proposed to establish refrigeration and transportation. It is said that the authorities will adopt and implement this plan. The plan is recorded below:

"China's fishery industry has been affected by the economic downturn, leading to increasing economic hardship in fishing villages and a falling price of fish. Aquatic products are not only subjected to the pressure of dumping by foreign goods, but also difficult to preserve due to their nature, making it impossible to transport and sell them elsewhere. Therefore, their price drop is more severe than other commodities. To save the situation, it is necessary to find ways to increase fish prices. The most effective way to increase fish prices is to prevent the import of foreign aquatic products and expand the sales of domestic fish. The former method is difficult to achieve because China's tariffs have not yet reached complete autonomy. The latter method is within our ability and should be carried out quickly to save the fishery industry from danger. Regarding this, the station has previously proposed a canned food manufacturing improvement plan, which has been approved for implementation. To implement this proposal and popularize the fish market, we will again propose refrigeration and transportation methods to keep fish fresh for transportation and sales to distant places. Everyone knows about the refrigeration method, but operators are limited to the coast, and very few have factories in the interior. Refrigerated transportation is even less developed. This is indeed a major reason why fish sales are not smooth and fish prices are low. In fact, inland areas of this province, such as Jinhua and Quzhou, only have freshwater fish because marine fish cannot be transported in, and fish prices are as high as two jiao per catty, while saltwater fish prices on the coast are only seven or eight fen, a difference of several times. In other coastal areas, such as Yongjia, fish prices are higher than Dinghai and Ningbo because they are farther from the fishing grounds. If refrigeration and transportation are established, allowing cheap marine fish to be transported everywhere, then on the one hand, the sales of fish will be expanded, and the value of fish catches will naturally increase, benefiting fishermen directly. On the other hand, inland residents can enjoy cheaper and more nutritious marine products. This province does not have many livestock products, but it is extremely rich in aquatic products. If refrigeration and transportation are established, people can eat fish to replace livestock. The economic benefits to the province will be significant. The methods and budget are listed below: Establish a refrigeration warehouse in each of Ningbo, Hangzhou, Jinhua, and Nanchang, together with the station's existing Dinghai refrigeration warehouse, for a total of five refrigeration warehouses. Each warehouse will have an average capacity of approximately 300,000 catties, capable of storing a total of 1.5 million catties of fish. During the fish season, when fish prices are low, collect large quantities of fish in Dinghai and Ningbo and transport them to various refrigeration warehouses for storage, waiting for prices to rise. The fish stored in the Dinghai and Ningbo warehouses will not only be transported to Hangzhou, Jinhua, and Nanchang at any time, but also sold to various coastal areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang when fish prices are high. Refrigerated fish in Hangzhou will be sold exclusively downstream of the Qiantang River. Fish in Jinhua will be sold upstream of the Qiantang River. Fish in Nanchang will be sold in various areas of Jiangxi Province. For transportation methods, ordinary ships will be temporarily used in coastal areas. For land transportation of each warehouse, it is proposed to request Hangzhou-Ningbo and Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railways to jointly set up an insulated car, which can carry about 40,000 catties of fish. As for the transportation between inland towns, it is proposed to set up a green car in each of the Hangzhou, Jinhua, and Nanchang warehouses to transport fish. Budget: Operating costs: Total expenditure of 217,200.00 yuan. Recurring costs and operating expenses: Total expenditure of 247,360.00 yuan. Business income: Total income of 285,000.00 yuan."

Suzhou National Goods Promotion Movement

The Wuxian National Goods Year Implementation Committee, in order to promote national goods, held a National Goods Promotion Conference at 1:00 PM on the 15th on the second floor of the National Goods Shopping Center in Beiju. National goods merchants swore an oath. To arouse public interest in using national goods, a national goods speech competition was held, followed by a national goods fashion show. Eleven participants participated in the show, all of whom were social flowers in Suzhou. At that time, national goods manufacturers such as the Nanyang Brothers Tobacco Company distributed national goods products. Participants were very enthusiastic. A national goods food exhibition was also set up at the Yong'an National Goods Shopping Center for people to visit. The Dachunghua National Goods Company in Guanqian Street also participated in the promotion at the beginning, but suddenly stopped halfway. On the same day, representatives from various schools in Suzhou were dispatched to inspect whether the national goods shopping centers were purely national goods.

Branch Line Laborer Cuts the Station Master

Zhang Mutao, the station master of the Suzhou Railway Station on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway, was attacked by a railway branch line laborer, Yang Licai. Yang Licai was suspended from his duties by the railway bureau due to poor performance. Harboring resentment, he set up at 7:00 PM on the 14th and, armed with a sharp axe, cut station master Zhang's hands and arms in many places at Zhang's residence on the Qianwanli Bridge. The rickshaw puller successfully captured the assailant Yang Licai and sent him to the police station for investigation. After being injured, Zhang Mutao was immediately sent to the Gengsheng Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the injuries were superficial and not life-threatening.

Wuxi Smuggled Coal from Liujiang Transported to Wuxi

Smuggled coal from Liujiang, Linyu County, Hebei, was sold by unscrupulous merchants from Chengwu counties who organized a distribution center to sell to the interior. Ruikang transported 3,000 tons of smuggled coal to Jiangyin. After several twists and turns, it has been unloaded. However, the people of Chengwu are extremely excited. The chambers of commerce and coal industry guilds of each county have respectively informed their colleagues to refuse to sell it. Yuanda Coal Company in this county even sent someone to Cheng to negotiate the sale of smuggled coal. On the day before yesterday, 500 tons were unloaded from the warehouse near Bao'an Road in Jiangyin and loaded into fourteen barges. It was loaded and transported to Wuxi at 4:00 PM. The Jiangyin Coal Industry Guild quickly sent a telegram to the Wuxi Coal Industry Guild to pay attention. Yesterday (the 15th), the smuggled coal arrived at Wuxi but had not yet been unloaded. The customs inspection office in this county has dispatched personnel to investigate the truth and deal with it.

Silk Factories Prepare to Start Operations

The overseas silk market has been soaring in the past week because of the start of the American summer sales and insufficient inventory, leading to smooth sales. The Shanghai silk market has also been rising in price for days. Because of the rising silk market overseas, silk manufacturers in this county unanimously expect higher prices. The number of sales has been very high in recent days. Moreover, with the listing of spring cocoons this year, the factories that have stopped production are preparing to start operations. The Silk Factory Association held an extraordinary meeting yesterday afternoon to discuss the issue of the factory opening. It was resolved that the association should notify the factories preparing to start operations to send the names of shareholders and managers, the names of representatives attending the association, the number of silk cars, and the amount of capital to the association for registration within five days for verification and consultation. At the same time, the local business tax bureau sent two official letters to the Silk Factory Association, urging them to convene their colleagues as soon as possible to truthfully declare the business tax within five days for verification. After the Silk Factory Association approved the letter, it has been forwarded to each factory for compliance and reported before June 20.

Changzhou Jiangdu Overturned by Wind

Wuyi No. 1 Yidu Ferry boat of Yinshakou in the third district of Wujin County. On the 13th, it followed the practice of carrying passengers to the port of Jiangbei. When sailing, it carried more than 20 passengers. When sailing to the east Xin'gang area of Jiangbei boundary in the river, it was about 10 o'clock. Suddenly, the sky was covered, the wind was strong, and heavy rain suddenly fell. The river waves suddenly rose. The shed of the Yidu ferry boat was broken by the storm, and the boat capsized. All 20 passengers fell into the water. Fortunately, a Zhenjiang Shenji ship passed by the place and rushed to rescue them. More than 10 of the people who were rescued were rescued and taken to Jiangbei to return to their hometowns. The rest who were missing could not be salvaged. When the wind and rain calmed down, they tried to salvage the overturned boat. A middle-aged man and woman were found in the boat, both of whom had drowned, which was very tragic. The Yidu ferry boat was driven back to Yinshakou. The head of the township, Sun Yuanzhang, submitted a report to the Procuratorate of the local court about the accident and the discovery of the corpses. Prosecutor Guan Junjie went to investigate the situation on the 15th.

Jiaxing Agricultural Warehouse Closed

Since the current manager Shen Xianheng presided over the Jiaxing County Farmers Bank, he has been planning to develop the business with all his strength. Therefore, offices have been established in various towns, and agricultural warehouses have been established, which has greatly facilitated the mortgage of agricultural products by villagers. Now, because the summer season is approaching, the agricultural products stored in the warehouse should be forced to be redeemed. The business meeting decided to close all strict agricultural warehouses in Youchegang, Xincheng, Xinpu, Wangdian and other places from the 16th. The goods that have not been redeemed will be extended to the summer solstice, and will be auctioned and compensated after the expiration date. On the other hand, the bank will consider the local situation and organize the storage of agricultural products for mortgages, so that farmers can temporarily use beans, grass seeds, vegetable seeds, and local yarn for storage and mortgage.

Yangzhou Yangjingjingkou Section Open to Traffic

The section of the Yangjing Highway from Yangzhou to Xiannv Town has been very convenient for travelers since it was opened to traffic on the 31st of last month. Now, the roadbed from Jingjiang to Kouan has been built, and it will be opened to traffic on the 16th. The entire line to traffic will still take some time because all the bridges between Kouan and Xiannv Town have not yet been completed.

Pinghu Friction at the Zhen Lantern Festival Caused Trouble

Xindai Town in this county was eager to catch up after the urban area held a lantern parade three times to promote the prohibition of opium smoking. It contacted various agencies and tied up countless colorful lanterns. The townspeople of the town were accustomed to playing magical dramas and welcoming gods at the fair. When they heard about the lantern parade, the townspeople almost all persuaded them to join. So, tigers, leopards, lions, elephants, dragons, all kinds of lanterns, weird and strange, have nothing to do with the prohibition of opium smoking. The shooting stars and firecrackers used for worshipping gods were added, and a large rack of flames was released in the Nan Niu Chang in the middle of the city. The north of the field was directly opposite a bridge. The crowd all wanted to squeeze onto the bridge to watch. There were already more than a hundred people on the bridge. They were squeezed back and forth and could not avoid it, so they refused to exert force. Suddenly, the crowd was noisy, and the stone railings on the bridge, along with the audience, fell into the water. The number of injured is unknown. It is only rumored that seven people were the most seriously injured. The next day, it was changed to be held in Cangji Baitou. There were even more ignorant people watching the fireworks, and the surrounding crops were completely trampled, causing no small loss.

Haizhou A Rebellious Son Killed His Biological Mother

Jiang Xiaobo, a resident of Wuxiaoyuan in the third district of Guanyun County, is now in his forties. His profession is as a boatman. Because his business has been depressed recently, he has been heavily in debt. He sold his original sailboat, with a selling price of 165 yuan. His mother, Zhang, is over 60 years old. She usually relies on boat life. Now that it has been sold, she is not only helpless, but also has no place to settle her clothes and coffin in the future. She asked her son Xiaobo to ask for the price of the boat to be used as the cost of clothes and coffins. However, Xiaobo refused to give her a penny, causing the mother and son to quarrel. Xiaobo hated his mother for asking him for money, and at night the other day, he held a kitchen knife and killed his mother. After the incident, Xiaobo wanted to escape, but was discovered by his neighbors, who tied Xiaobo and sent him to the third district office. Lu District Chief has prepared a document today to send him to the county government for legal action.

Because the Dragon Boat Festival is approaching, the commercial accounts in Hangzhou City need to be settled. Xiaoshan Silkworm Cocoon Market Sets Fixed Closing Date

Xiaoshan is a silk-producing area. This year, silkworm farmers have produced a large quantity of green cocoons. There are a total of twenty-seven "Lan Hang" [silk filature guilds] in the county. The cocoon markets that purchase local varieties of cocoons have already stopped weighing and purchasing. The cocoon markets that purchase improved varieties started weighing and purchasing on the 1st and will continue until the 10th, a total of ten days. It is planned to uniformly stop weighing and purchasing from the 15th. However, the goods arriving this session are crowded, and each cocoon market has exceeded the original registered amount. Furthermore, because of the closing of the local cocoon markets, there is still a large quantity of fresh cocoons in the countryside, so they can only reel silk themselves. Also, the cocoon price was initially high but later became low, and the villagers suffered great losses. If methods are not devised to provide relief, more and more households will become discouraged. The future of the silk industry will definitely not be optimistic.

Fifteenth Health and Hygiene Campaign Opens Yesterday Morning at the People's Education Center

Director Li Leads a Major Clean-up with Broom in Hand. The Focus of This Campaign is Children

The Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association, the Municipal Health Bureau, the Public Concession Health Department, and forty-two organizations jointly organized the Fifteenth Health and Hygiene Campaign. It opened at 10:00 AM yesterday at the People's Education Center on Wenmiao Road in Ximen. First, Mayor Wu, representing Director Li Tingan, performed the ribbon-cutting ceremony, followed immediately by the opening ceremony. Then, Director Li and others led police officers, security teams, Boy Scouts, and service personnel from various districts in a parade and major cleanup. The details are recorded below:

Venue Arrangement

The scale of this Health and Hygiene Campaign is grand. The Party and national flags are crossed in front of the main gate, adorned with pine and cypress, and below is the artistic inscription of the four characters "Health and Hygiene Campaign." Upon entering, one sees health advertisements, colorful in red and green. At the middle gate bridge, three advertising kiosks are erected by the New Asia Pharmaceutical Factory and the Wuhe Factory. On the left side of the open space is the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Health Exhibition area, and on the right is the auditorium. The walkways are fenced off with bamboo railings to conform to the New Life Movement's rules of walking. Finally, there is the Public Concession Health Department exhibition. There is a decorated archway on the walkway in front of the Dacheng Hall, with the four characters "Protect Our Health" inscribed by Mayor Wu, next to a couplet that reads, "Do not allow sorrow and joy to reach extremes; one should ensure a balanced diet." In addition, security team police officers and Boy Scouts from the Civil Girls' High School are also maintaining order in the venue.

Participating Representatives

Those attending the opening ceremony included Mayor Wu (represented by Li Yan'an), Tong Hangbai of the Municipal Party Department, Pan Gongzhan of the New Life Movement Promotion Association, Li Tingan, Director of the Health Bureau, Cai Jingjun, Director of the Public Security Bureau (represented by Hong Qi), Wu Xingya, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau (represented by Zhang Binghui), Ji Zhangjian, Commander of the Security General Corps (represented by Lin Zhisheng), Zhu Erden, Director of the Public Concession Health Department (Qiong Siden), Zhou Xuexiang of the General Labor Union, Cao Zhigong of the Pharmaceutical Industry Association, Mao Zhixiang of the Dental Association, Tu Kaizheng of the New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, Li Xiaohua of the Anti-Smoking Investigation Commissioner's Office, Li Weiye of the Wusong Health Office, Yun Jihua of the South Shanghai Health Office, and over a thousand people including conference staff members Zhu Jiarang, Shen Gao, Zhu Xiaochun, Wu Zhongyao, and Yin Yong.

(International Photograph)

Opening Ceremony

At the second gate of the venue, there was a colored ribbon, guarded by Girl Scouts holding sticks. As the time approached 10:00 AM, Director Li cut it open, and the opening ceremony was declared open. Immediately afterward, Committee Member Tong, Section Chief Shen, Section Chief Zhang, and representatives from all sectors successively inspected the venue. First, the slogan "Health and Life" in large red characters caught the eye. They then inspected the venue in five departments. After inspecting the dental hygiene section, the representatives proceeded to the auditorium to take their seats. The opening program began with the Public Security Bureau Music Corps playing music, singing the Party song, and giving the highest salute to the portrait of the late President. After the chairman respectfully read the President's will, President Li began his speech, which was broadcast throughout the entire venue through loudspeakers. Subsequently, Committee Member Tong, Director Pan, and Qiong Siden, the representative of the Public Concession Health Department, also gave speeches. Finally, male and female students from Huaguang Elementary School sang health songs, followed by music and photography.

General Content of Speeches

Chairman Li Tingan reported, in brief, "Ladies and gentlemen, our Shanghai Fifteenth Health and Hygiene Campaign is organized by the New Life Movement Promotion Association, the Health Bureau, the Public Concession Health Department, and over forty organizations. The difference between this session and previous sessions is the cooperation between this association and various organizations such as the New Life Movement Association. Preparations have taken months to achieve today's phenomenon, all thanks to the enthusiastic support of various organizations. This is the special feature of this conference. Because this year is Children's Year, all work is focused on children. However, the program has been researched and found to be more extensive than previous sessions, including: 1. Infant Health Competition, 2. Children's Hygiene Competition, 3. Children's Clothing Competition, 4. Mother's Day, 5. Anti-Spitting Campaign, 6. Health Guidance, 7. Fly Eradication Campaign, 8. Centralized Training for Food Establishments. As for the duration of the conference, it is also longer than before. The 16th is Children's Toy Hygiene Guidance, the 17th is Children's Dietary Hygiene Guidance, the 18th is Entertainment, the 19th is Children's Health Competition, the 20th is Sunday, the 21st is Children's Hygiene Speech Competition, the 22nd is a day of rest, the 23rd is Factory Hygiene, the 24th is Children's Life Guidance, the 25th is Anti-Spitting, the 26th is Children's Oral Hygiene, the 27th is Mother's Day, the 28th is Youth Day, the 29th is rest, and the 30th is the closing ceremony. As for the issue of funding, it is different from the past. Previously, the Municipal Government allocated 1,040 yuan, and the shortfall was raised freely. This year, there is only 500 yuan of funding, but there are many participating organizations, and advertising costs also take up a considerable amount, but it can generally be maintained." Next, Tong Hangbai gave a speech, in brief, "Distinguished guests, today is the first day of the Health and Hygiene Campaign. I am participating on behalf of the Municipal Party Department. The Health and Hygiene Campaign is one of the New Life Movement, and it is closely related to the survival of the nation. Looking at the extreme danger facing China today, many people are still unaware of hygiene. Neglecting the Health and Hygiene Campaign makes it difficult to engage in the national salvation movement. From this, one can understand." Finally, the representative of the Public Concession Health Department gave a speech, the content of which is omitted for brevity.

Parade and Street Cleaning

After the photography, the procession was organized. Various organizations and representatives, as well as service groups from various districts and the public, numbering about a thousand people, each with a broom, set off towards Ximen. Director Li, Committee Member Tong, and others led the way, with the Public Security Bureau band leading the vanguard. Arriving at the Ximen Memorial Tower, brooms were waved in unison, a spectacular sight. The parade participants took the area around the tower, which was hung with a banner that read "Shanghai Health and Hygiene Campaign Major Cleanup," as the final destination and dispersed in all directions.

Torrential Rain

As soon as the conference ended, a sudden wind and rainstorm struck, and pedestrians were unable to escape, getting drenched. The Health and Hygiene Campaign venue, constructed from reed mats and oiled paper, was attacked by the storm, and many of the exhibits were also damp. According to the manager, fortunately, the exhibits were not damaged. After the rain cleared and the sky cleared, the exhibition resumed as usual.

The first part of the exhibition, regarding physiological hygiene, included detailed explanations of the ten-month-old fetus model. Disease prevention and rules for healthy habits were also available for public viewing.

Today's Program

Today is Children's Toy Hygiene Guidance Day, organized by the China Benevolent Children's Society. In addition to lectures in the auditorium, Municipal Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Finance Bureau Director Xu Fu, and Zhu Erden (Dr. G. H. Gordon) of the Public Concession Health Department have been invited to broadcast lectures on the radio.

Completion of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Loan. Fund Management Committee Meets Yesterday

The first meeting of the Bonded Trustee Committee for the completion of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway's 6% Gold Bond Loan was held at 3:00 PM on June 15 at the Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration office. Attendees included Chairman Zhang Gongquan, Minister of Railways, Committee members Song Ziliang, representative of the China Construction Bank, Davidson, representative of the China-British Bank, and Safu Jun and Lin Zhaotang, representatives of the Ministry of Railways. Pan Guangjiong, Chief Secretary of the Ministry of Railways, Huang Boqiao, Director of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, and He Molin, Deputy Director, were also present. The heads of the accounting office of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, Si Douya, and Deputy Director Mo Jiefu served as secretaries. The meeting was chaired by Minister Zhang, and the order of the meeting was as follows: 1. Chairman's opening remarks, 2. Approval of the rules and regulations of the Bonded Trustee Committee, 3. The Director of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, designated by the Minister of Railways, has the authority to deposit the loan proceeds in the bank and should be filed for record, 4. Acceptance of the accounting officer recommended by the banking syndicate and submission to the Minister of Railways for appointment (Mo Jiefu, Deputy Director of the Accounting Office of the Shanghai-Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, was recommended by the banking syndicate and concurrently appointed as the acting director of the accounting office), 5. Grant the secretary the authority to purchase record books and other urgent expenses. The speeches of Chairman Zhang and the representatives of the China Construction Bank and the China-British Bank are recorded below.

Chairman Zhang's Speech

"Gentlemen, I am deeply honored to be the chairman of the first meeting of the Bonded Trustee Committee for the completion of the 6% Gold Bond Loan for the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway of the National Government of China. This loan is the result of the sincere efforts of the China-British Bank and the China Construction Bank. After several twists and turns in the past and in the current difficult situation, the bonds were finally issued. I am deeply grateful for their sincere cooperation and courageous handling. The Ministry of Railways, in its determination to restore railway credit, took the opportunity to negotiate this loan agreement to establish a deeper friendship with the China-British Bank and a new and closer relationship with the China Construction Bank, which is very gratifying. The organization and establishment of this committee is very different from previous methods, which is sufficient to indicate the deep mutual trust and cooperation between the two sides. We engaged in the railway industry feel that the reason why the four banks, HSBC, Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, cooperated so closely is that the driving force is not the pursuit of ordinary commercial profits, but the firm belief in railway investment. This matter is tantamount to obtaining a resolution of confidence for those in charge of railways. I believe that the issuance of bonds is extremely important. We have not publicly issued railway bonds for many years. Those who purchase bonds must be able to clearly distinguish between the market price and the true value of the bonds. The true value of the bonds does not fluctuate with the ups and downs of the market price, but must be viewed in terms of their nature, that is, whether railway administration is sound and whether debts are fulfilled on time. Only by earnestly implementing these points can we hope that the public will actively subscribe. We have high expectations for the construction of domestic railways because the recovery of the Chinese national economy is extremely important for railways. The railways in China are not only the center of the economy but also a profitable investment. Given China's vast territory and abundant production, the existing railway lines are definitely not enough to meet the demand. Therefore, Chinese railways are a great investment market. I hope that the administration of the railway bureau can achieve the greatest efficiency with the most economical expenditure and that this committee will faithfully perform its duties and gain public trust, just as the price of the old Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway bonds rose to 102 yuan. In short, China needs railways, and the opportunity is unmatched elsewhere in the world. I believe that this loan is nothing more than the vanguard of many similar investments."

Committee Member Song's Speech

The main idea is that today's first meeting of the committee is extremely important. It is the first time for China and foreign countries to cooperate and jointly invest in Chinese railway construction, and China expects many railways to be built. It is hoped that all future projects can be carried out in this joint investment method. The committee does not hope to be a supervisory body, but wishes to assist the railway bureau. The current situation of the railway bureau is very good, and it is hoped that it can further increase revenue and reduce expenditure in the future, so that finances can be further consolidated. Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces are the richest regions in China, and the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways are located in a connecting position. Unfortunately, a section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway has not yet been connected, which is a pity. Therefore, the name of this loan is to complete the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway. It is hoped that the construction project will be completed soon and the entire railway will be connected.

Davidson's Speech

The main idea is that he was deeply impressed and interested in listening to the chairman's speech just now. The railway loan has been interrupted for many years. The establishment of this railway loan is tantamount to further consolidating the existing friendship between China and the United Kingdom. This loan is the vanguard of the same loan in the future. My intention is the same as the chairman's. The signing of this loan agreement and the issuance of bonds on the market are clearly an expression of the China-British Bank's trust in the National Government of China and the Ministry of Railways. The current loan agreement is extremely important. We must strive for economic efficiency in construction costs and strive for great effectiveness. In the future, we must also strive to fulfill principal and interest payments as scheduled. I feel that under the chairman's leadership, all financial difficulties can be resolved. I wish you success.

Sun Jiaze did not travel with me. I plan to stay in Shanghai for a short time and then go to Nanjing.

Tang's Remarks

Tang Haian previously went to Guangdong by order of Finance Minister Kong to discuss the silver dollar system and anti-smuggling issues. This time, he returned north with a plan for reform and will present it to Finance Minister Kong for guidance. According to Tang, regarding the silver dollar system, the results of this trip to Guangdong were quite satisfactory, and a specific plan for reforming the silver dollar system was drafted and submitted to Finance Minister Kong for instruction in preparation for implementation. The silver stored in Guangdong will be transferred to the central government in exchange for legal tender to avoid outflow. Tang was unwilling to express any views on the current situation and anti-smuggling issues.

Representatives from All Sectors Commemorate the Passing of the Late President in Guangzhou This Morning

10:00 AM at the Municipal Party Headquarters Auditorium

Guomin News reports that today is the fourteenth anniversary of the passing of the late President in Guangzhou. The Municipal Party Headquarters of this city is scheduled to convene a memorial service for representatives from all sectors at 10:00 AM today. All cities and towns are required to fly flags at half-mast for commemoration. The authorities of the Chinese and Foreign Concessions have taken strict precautions to prevent disturbances to public order by unscrupulous elements. The following is a brief history of the passing of the late President: In 1922 (Gregorian calendar), the late President moved his troops from Guangxi to the Northern Expedition. Because Chen Jiongming colluded with Wu Peifu and others to obstruct the rear, he returned to Guangzhou in April. Chen fled to Huizhou and instigated his subordinates to launch an armed attack on the Presidential Palace on June 16. The late President then boarded the Yongfeng warship and led the navy to quell the rebellion, confronting Chen in the Guangzhou River for about a month. He telegraphed the troops who had entered Jiangxi to return to Guangdong to quell the rebellion, but they were unsuccessful. On August 9, he left Guangzhou for Shanghai.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Prohibits Blank Sale Transactions

Transactions Must be Signed by Exchange Brokers

Nanjing Telephone, In order to prohibit blank sale and purchase transactions in the Shanghai Stock Exchange, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce ordered the Shanghai Stock Exchange Federation that thereafter, the brokers of each exchange should, for the sale and purchase entrusted by the trustee, whether buying or selling, or delivery, should pass through their respective exchange, and the transaction order should be completed by the exchange in accordance with the provisions of the internal statute, and signed by both parties' brokers to complete the transaction, and must not be violated. Telephone Association Asks Chamber of Commerce to Propose at the General Assembly to Discuss Telephone Rate Increases

Advocating a Uniform Three Cents Per Call

The Special District Telephone Problem Committee, considering that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce of this city will hold a general meeting of members on the 20th of this month, sent a letter to the Chamber yesterday, asking that the issue of telephone rate increases by the Shanghai Telephone Company be included in the agenda for discussion at the general meeting in order to seek a solution. The original letter is recorded below: "Regarding the issue of telephone rate increases in the Special District, although the public associations of this city have repeatedly declared their opposition, the company, relying on the operating franchise granted by the Public Works Department, intends to increase the official interest rate by one cent and refuses to accept it, resulting in a stalemate that has not yet been resolved. Previously, the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Public Concession sent a letter stating that the solution to the case requires first investigating the company's income to determine whether it exceeds the official interest rate by one cent. Our association has informed users to collect bills separately in preparation for the entire negotiation. However, telephones are a tool for commercial communication. The illegal rate increase by the company this time has had a deep impact on commerce. Your Chamber is the hub of commerce, and it has previously sent a letter stating that it would submit the issue to the general meeting of members on June 20 for discussion. As the meeting date is approaching, we are sending another letter requesting that the case be included in the agenda for discussion in order to reach a uniform rate of three cents per call, regardless of the basic rate or the number of calls exceeding the limit. Furthermore, the Public Works Department's unauthorized rate increase for public utilities without obtaining the consent of taxpayers is a disregard for public sentiment and should be discussed together in order to safeguard the public interests of citizens in the Special District. The matter is of great importance and we hope you will pay attention to it."

Silver and Money Industries Announce Refusal to Accept Loans Secured by Smuggled Goods

Those Who Knowingly Accept Tax-Evading Goods Will be Severely Punished in Accordance with the Criminal Law on Receiving Stolen Goods

The Shanghai Kouqian (Buckle Money) and Silver Industry Association received an order from the Ministry not to accept loans secured by tax-evading goods. Yesterday, it issued a public announcement to its member firms to comply with the following document: "Yesterday, we received a Yuan Telegram from the Ministry of Finance, addressed to the Banking Association and the Money Industry Association. An investigation has revealed that receiving and purchasing tax-evading goods should be subject to criminal penalties in accordance with the Criminal Law on Receiving Stolen Goods, which has been presented to the Executive Yuan for approval and forwarded for record and notification. Recent confidential reports indicate that many smugglers are mortgaging tax-evading smuggled goods to silver and money firms to facilitate transportation. If firms accept such mortgages, it is equivalent to receiving tax-evading goods and is a criminal offense. Strict warnings should be given to prevent this. Therefore, we are issuing this telegram to inform all firms that when accepting goods as collateral, if the goods are imported, in addition to providing the storage receipt and bill of lading at the original port of import, a tax payment receipt obtained from the customs office should also be provided. For goods transported from the original port of import to various places, in addition to providing the storage receipt and bill of lading, a certificate from the local Chamber of Commerce or trade association should also be obtained, stating that the goods have been issued a transportation permit by the customs office and approved for transportation and registered with the association. If the above certificate cannot be obtained and there is suspicion of tax evasion, the bill of lading and storage receipt should be detained and reported to the local government or directly submitted to the Ministry for investigation. If any firm knowingly accepts tax-evading goods as collateral, the managers of the firm will be severely punished in accordance with the Criminal Law on Receiving Stolen Goods to deter wrongdoing once the facts are verified. In addition to sending separate telegrams, we are issuing this telegram for compliance and notification to all member firms (banks) for your information."

Zhejiang Federation Submits a Request to the Zhejiang Provincial Government: Please Exempt Silk Cocoons from Detention

Detailed Explanation of Dissatisfaction with Central Pricing Due to Three Reasons

Grant Passage First to Those Priced Above 19 Yuan

Sample Testing Only for Those Below to Reduce Losses

The Joint Federation of Zhejiang Provincial Silk Cocoon Industry Associations of Lianzhu Lane, Avenue Edward VII, Shanghai, after repeatedly receiving letters from various local industry associations reporting that the Management Office of the Cocoon Control Committee of Zhejiang Province is detaining all spring silk cocoons that do not meet the central price,

resulting in unbearable losses, the federation, based on the situation, yesterday submitted a document to Chairman Huang of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, stating, "Submitted for the matter of requesting exemption from detention. Our association has repeatedly received letters from various local industry associations stating that this year's spring cocoons, those whose purchase price does not meet the central price, are uniformly detained by the Management Office of the Control Committee, resulting in unbearable losses, etc., entrusting our association to request release and transportation. Our association investigated the situation and found approximately three points, which we respectfully present to your Excellency: The quality is too poor. The original price list was based on the degree of silk reeling loss as the standard. The difference in silk reeling loss this year compared to last year is such that each picul has increased by as much as one hundred and several tens of catties, some have increased by seventy or eighty catties, and the minimum is an increase of forty or fifty catties. This was truly unexpected by the Control Committee when setting the price. With such poor quality, how can the price be increased?

Deqing, Chongde, Haining, and other counties have historically had silk reeling losses that were not very good, but this year they are even worse. Merchants, in order to preserve their capital, followed the pricing table set by the Control Committee and calculated the purchase price. How could they suppress the price? Yet the Control Committee is detaining all cocoons priced below twenty-one yuan, regardless of how many cents or jiao, even though there was no such method before, and there was no clear order given in advance. This is the first reason why exemption from detention should be requested. The price of silk is gradually decreasing. When the Control Committee set the cocoon price, it was based on a silk price of 665 taels. Now, however, the price of silk in overseas markets and among domestic users has fallen below 600 yuan for higher grades, and only 540 or 550 yuan for lower grades. The current silk price

is different from the silk price when the cocoon price was set

by more than one hundred yuan, or fifty or sixty yuan. Merchants, seeing this market situation, how can they not consider costs? Moreover, business is originally for profit, and it is not appropriate to save people from the well. The rise and fall of the silk price, and the size of the cocoon price, are dictated by the facts, and there is absolutely no intention to greedily seek cheap prices or hinder the interests of silk cocoon farmers. The Control Committee, being aware of the ways of the world, directly strikes down the silk cocoon merchants, which is indirectly striking down the rural areas. Why only consider the silk cocoon farmers and not at all consider the silk cocoon merchants? Being biased towards one side, how can it be reconciled? This is the second reason why exemption from detention should be requested. Silk cocoon farmers are eager to sell. Good quality cocoons, even if the price is increased, farmers are still unwilling to sell them easily. Only inferior cocoons are rejected by the silk cocoon merchants, and the farmers return again and again, even begging to be bought in order to sell their goods for cash, and some even asking others to intercede

and voluntarily lower the price.

Whether the cocoons are good or bad, silk cocoon merchants pay the same improvement fee and the same packaging and drying fees. Is it better to buy good cocoons or bad cocoons? Even though silk cocoon merchants have the power, they would never willingly buy bad cocoons. The fact that they do so is out of consideration for the livelihood of the silk cocoon farmers, and it is truly unavoidable, resulting in a price that does not meet the central price. This is precisely the hardship of the silk cocoon merchants, and not their black hearts. Being personally involved in the situation, one can understand it clearly. This is the third reason why exemption from detention should be requested. Based on the above three points, the Control Committee's severe actions truly disregard the difficulties of the merchants. Merchants who buy cocoons urgently need to transport them to Shanghai to pledge for funds to repay loans, urgently need to process them into silk to deliver futures contracts, and urgently want to reel and select

to maintain workers.

If sixty percent are not allowed to be shipped, and forty percent are still retained, silk cocoon merchants have no choice but to send people to watch over them, increasing expenses by one share, which increases costs by one share. In this time of sluggish market conditions, how can they bear this loss? The original Control Committee's talk of sample testing was nothing more than to clarify the truth and prevent price suppression. However, the extent of silk reeling loss this year is truly alarming. The silk reeling loss tested by various silk mills has reached as high as 670 or 680 catties on the Sima scale. The most common, such as Deqing, Chongde, Haining, and other silk producing areas, are generally around 600 catties. Compared to last year, the hidden loss has increased by more than 100 yuan, or 70 or 80 yuan, or 50 or 60 yuan per picul of silk. Taking one silk mill as an example, for 500 piculs of silk, it is necessary to increase the purchase of 500 piculs of cocoons. The value of these 500 piculs of

dry cocoons

is nearly 50,000 yuan. How can they sustain such hidden losses? Silk cocoon merchants have suffered disastrous losses for years, and the rural areas have gone bankrupt as a result. The government is already struggling to provide relief and maintenance, yet it uses pressure to bind the silk cocoon merchants, crushing them, as if fearing it is not enough, suddenly accusing them of price suppression. The silk cocoon merchants are left to await death with their hands tied. Is this truly the blessing of the country? Even if the sample testing clarifies the situation and avoids punishment, who will compensate the silk cocoon merchants for their losses? Our association is a silk cocoon industry organization, and we respectfully request that the Control Committee respect its own set cocoon price table, and grant passage first to all those priced above 19 yuan and 29 cents. For those below that price, then conduct sample testing to reduce the suffering of the silk cocoon merchants. We hope that your Excellency will impartially handle this matter. This is truly for the public good. Respectfully submitted to Huang, Chairman of Zhejiang Province.

Putuo Combined Route

Sino-Japanese Wireless Telephone

Shanghai-Sapporo Call Today

After the Sino-Japanese wireless telephone between Shanghai and Tokyo opened on February 15, the Sino-Japanese wireless telephone between Shanghai and Sapporo, Hokkaido, will open today. The details are recorded separately below:

Opening Today The Sino-Japanese international wireless telephone initiated by the International Telecommunications Bureau opened between Shanghai and Tokyo on February 15. Since Sapporo, Hokkaido, Japan, is also a commercial center, the bureau has been actively preparing after the Tokyo call, and it has now been completed. The Shanghai-Sapporo call is scheduled to open at 9:00 AM today. As for other places such as Yokohama and Osaka, the bureau is also actively preparing, and calls should be available in the near future.

Types of Calls The types of calls in both places are divided into (A) Person-to-Person Calls (must first state your name and telephone number, and specify the telephone number and person to call), (B) Number-to-Number Calls (do not specify the telephone number and person to call), (C) Messenger Calls (to call someone at a place who does not have a telephone and requires the telephone company to send someone to notify them).

Procedures and Time Those in the city who want to call Sapporo and do not know the situation can dial 41000 to inquire. Those in the concessions can first dial "02" and call 41000 to inquire. When calling, dial "03" in the special district and "40" in the city to register, state the type of call you want to make, and wait for the telephone company to notify you to speak after the connection is made. Call time is from 9:00 AM to 4:00 PM.

Stipulated Prices The stipulated price for calls in both places is 15 yuan for each three minutes. If it is less than three minutes, it is still calculated as three minutes. For each additional minute or less, add 5 yuan. As for after the connection, if the other party does not want to talk or the person being searched for cannot be found, it will be canceled, and the cancellation fee is 1.5 yuan per time.

New Standards for Tea Inspection Implemented on July 1

A Total of Four Points Approved by the Ministry of Industry

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, in order to promote the development of tea exports, has revised the export inspection standards for tea and decided to implement them starting from July 1st. These new standards for tea inspection and enforcement measures were decided at the Tea Standards Conference and approved by the Ministry of Industry, including the Inspection method for ash content, which has long been consistent between the Shanghai and Hankou bureaus. However, the moisture inspection, which used to use the weighing method, was difficult to adjust due to excessive oven use. As a result, the inspection results were inconsistent. Now, the simplified volumetric method of Hoffmann is used to ensure that the inspection results are consistent with each other. As for the standards for red and green tea, it was agreed to continue to use the same models as last year. In terms of moisture, the method was changed to the Hoffmann volumetric method. Compared with the old method, the actual difference is an average increase of 1.5 percent, so the numbers remain the same as last year and will not be changed. The measures to crack down on dyed tea are the same as last year. After several years of cracking down on dyed tea, the highest standard for dyeing tea has been reduced. This year, it has been decided to lower it again, and actively use yellow dye. If necessary, it is planned to cooperate with the local government to train a number of inspectors to go to various places to provide guidance. With regard to cracking down on substandard tea packaging, European and American tea merchants have repeatedly sent letters requesting attention. Chinese merchants also recognize the need for improvement. It has been decided to issue a notice to tea merchants that starting this year, they should add ten wooden strips to the existing tea boxes to ensure that the box shape does not change and is twice as strong.

They have already split into groups to inspect commerce, economy, education, etc. They are scheduled to leave Siam and return to China in early July and are expected to arrive in Shanghai in mid-July.

Post Office Provides its Own Postal Delivery Cars

Petitioning Various Highway Authorities to Provide Convenience

Since the space for carrying mail on long-distance buses is limited, the Ministry of Communications has decided to order the post office to provide its own cars to transport mail exclusively, and has petitioned the Executive Yuan to instruct the relevant highway authorities to provide full convenience when driving. "The transportation of mail by long-distance buses should strictly comply with the Postal Regulations and the Regulations on Transportation of Mail by Long-Distance Buses stipulated by the Ministry, and on February 18th of the 24th year of the Republic (1935), the relevant points to be observed by various provincial and municipal agencies, as well as public and private bus companies, for the transportation of mail were opened, and the 28th submission was submitted to the Executive Yuan and approved on February 23rd of the 24th year of the Republic (1935) with Instruction No. 594, stating, 'The submission has been noted and approved as requested in the submission. An order has been issued to various provincial and municipal governments to strictly comply with the instructions.' In order to improve the situation, it is necessary for the post office to, in addition to transportation by long-distance buses, consider the circumstances in various places and either provide its own cars or rent vehicles to transport mail exclusively on various highways, in order to expedite mail delivery. It is proposed to request the Executive Yuan to issue an order to various provincial and municipal governments, transferring it to various highway management agencies, to provide full convenience to the post office's own vehicles, or rented vehicles, that are exclusively transporting mail on the highway, and to inform the Chairman of the Military Commission of the Bashan Branch of the Kuomintang, as well as the National Economic Council, for review, in order to facilitate transportation. It is for the public benefit. Respectfully submitted to the Executive Yuan, Vice Minister of the Ministry of Communications, acting as minister Yu Feipeng."
